2017-08-15 19:36:07,099 p=29300 u=wtooles |  ERROR! failed at splitting arguments, either an unbalanced jinja2 block or quotes: msg="Public IP address is {{ "ip_address.stdout }}"

The error appears to have been in '/media/sf_git-repos/aCloudGuru-AdvancedCloudFormation-bill/ansible/change_fw.yaml': line 44, column 7, but may
be elsewhere in the file depending on the exact syntax problem.

The offending line appears to be:

    - debug: msg="Created instance id is {{ ec2_instance_id.stdout }}"
    - debug: msg="Public IP address is {{ "ip_address.stdout }}"
      ^ here
We could be wrong, but this one looks like it might be an issue with
missing quotes.  Always quote template expression brackets when they
start a value. For instance:

    with_items:
      - {{ foo }}

Should be written as:

    with_items:
      - "{{ foo }}"
